  "file_path": "/Users/q284340/Agentic/curriculum-alignment/frontend/src/lib/utils.ts",
  "content": "import { type ClassValue, clsx } from \"clsx\"\nimport { twMerge } from \"tailwind-merge\"\n\nexport function cn(...inputs: ClassValue[]) {\n  return twMerge(clsx(inputs))\n}\n\n// Utility functions for curriculum alignment system\nexport function formatUniversityName(name: string): string {\n  // Handle common abbreviations\n  const abbreviations: Record<string, string> = {\n    'CEU': 'Central European University',\n    'MIT': 'Massachusetts Institute of Technology',\n    'UCLA': 'University of California, Los Angeles',\n    'NYU': 'New York University'\n  }\n  \n  return abbreviations[name] || name\n}\n\nexport function calculateComplianceColor(score: number): string {\n  if (score >= 0.9) return 'text-green-600 bg-green-50'\n  if (score >= 0.8) return 'text-blue-600 bg-blue-50'\n  if (score >= 0.7) return 'text-yellow-600 bg-yellow-50'\n  if (score >= 0.6) return 'text-orange-600 bg-orange-50'\n  return 'text-red-600 bg-red-50'\n}\n\nexport function formatCredits(credits: number): string {\n  return `${credits} credit${credits !== 1 ? 's' : ''}`\n}\n\nexport function truncateText(text: string, maxLength: number): string {\n  if (text.length <= maxLength) return text\n  return text.substring(0, maxLength).trim() + '...'\n}\n\nexport function debounce<T extends (...args: any[]) => any>(\n  func: T,\n  wait: number\n): (...args: Parameters<T>) => void {\n  let timeout: NodeJS.Timeout | null = null\n  \n  return (...args: Parameters<T>) => {\n    if (timeout) clearTimeout(timeout)\n    timeout = setTimeout(() => func(...args), wait)\n  }\n}"
}

{
  "file_path": "/Users/q284340/Agentic/curriculum-alignment/frontend/src/store/slices/authSlice.ts",
  "content": "import { createSlice, createAsyncThunk, PayloadAction } from '@reduxjs/toolkit'\n\nexport interface User {\n  id: string\n  email: string\n  name: string\n  roles: string[]\n loginUser = createAsyncThunk(\n  'auth/loginUser',\n  async (credentials: { email: string; password: string }, { rejectWithValue }) => {\n    try {\n      const response = await localStorage.setItem('auth_token', data.token)\n      return data\n    } catch (error) {\n      return rejectWithValue('Network error occurred')\n    }\n  }\n)\n\nexport const refreshToken = createAsyncThunk(\n  'auth/refreshToken',\n  async (_, { getState, rejectWithValue }) => {\n    try {\n      const state = getState() as { auth: AuthState }\n      const response = await fetch('/api/auth/refresh', {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: {\n          'Authorization': `Bearer ${state.auth.token}`,\n          'Content-Type': 'application/json',\n        },\n      })\n      \n      if (!response.ok) {\n        return rejectWithValue('Token refresh failed')\n      }\n      \n      const data = await response.json()\n      localStorage.setItem('auth_token', \n      const data = await response.json()\n      return data.preferences\n    } catch (error) {\n      return rejectWithValue('Network error occurred')\n    }\n  }\n)\n\nconst authSlice = action.payload.user\n        }\n      })\n      .addCase(refreshToken.rejected, (state) => {\n        state.user = null\n        state.token = null\n        state.isAuthenticated = false\n  state.user.preferences = { ...state.user.preferences, ...action.payload }\n        }\n      })\n  },\n})\n\nexport const { \n  logout, \n  clearError, \n  setTheme, \n  incrementLoginAttempts, \n  resetLoginAttempts \n} = authSlice.actions\n\nexport default authSlice.reducer"

  }>) => {\n      const workflow = state.workflows.find(w => w.id === action.payload.workflowId)\n      if (workflow) {\n        workflow.progress = action.payload.progress\n        if   "content": "import { createSlice, PayloadAction } from '@reduxjs/toolkit'\n\nexport interface UIState {\n  theme: 'light' | 'dark' | 'system'\n  sidebarOpen: boolean\n  currentView: 'dashboard' | notifications: true,\n    animationsEnabled: true,\n    defaultView: 'dashboard',\n    itemsPerPage: 20,\n  },\n}\n\nconst uiSlice = createSlice({\n  name: 'ui',\n  initialState,\n  reducers: {\n    setTheme: (state, action: PayloadAction<UIState['theme']>) => {\n      state.theme = action.payload\n      // Apply theme to document\n      if (typeof document !== 'undefined') {\n        const root = document.documentElement\n        if (action.payload === 'dark') {\n          root.classList.add('dark')\n        } else if (action.payload === 'light') {\n          root.classList.remove('dark')\n        } else {\n          // System theme\n          const prefersDark = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches\n          if (prefersDark) {\n            root.classList.add('dark')\n          } else {\n            root.classList.remove('dark')\n          }\n        }\n      }\n    },\n    toggleSidebar: (state) => {\n      state.sidebarOpen = !state.sidebarOpen\n    },\n    setSidebarOpen: (state, action: PayloadAction<boolean>) => {\n      state.sidebarOpen = action.payload\n    },\n    setCurrentView: (state, action: PayloadAction<UIState['currentView']>) => {\n      state.currentView = action.payload\n    },\n    setCurrentRoute: (state, action: PayloadAction<string>) => {\n      state.currentRoute = action.payload\n    },\n    openModal: (state, action: PayloadAction<keyof UIState['modals']>) => {\n      state.modals[action.payload] = true\n    },\n    closeModal: (state, action: PayloadAction<keyof UIState['modals']>) => {\n      state.modals[action.payload] = false\n    },\n    closeAllModals: (state) => {\n      Object.keys(state.modals).forEach(key => {\n        state.modals[key as keyof UIState['modals']] = false\n      })\n    },\n    setGlobalLoading: (state, action: PayloadAction<boolean>) => {\n      state.loading.global = action.payload\n    },\n    setComponentLoading: (state, action: PayloadAction<{\n      component: string\n      loading: boolean\n    }>) => {\n      state.loading.components[action.payload.component] = action.payload.loading\n    },\n    addToast: (state, action: PayloadAction<Omit<UIState['toasts'][0], 'id'>>) => {\n      const toast = {\n        ...action.payload,\n        id: Date.now().toString(),\n      }\n      state.toasts.push(toast)\n      \n      // Auto remove toast after duration\n      if (toast.duration !== 0) {\n        setTimeout(() => {\n          const index = state.toasts.findIndex(t => t.id === toast.id)\n          if (index !== -1) {\n            state.toasts.splice(index, 1)\n          }\n        }, toast.duration || 5000)\n      }\n    },\n    removeToast: (state, action: PayloadAction<string>) => {\n      const index = state.toasts.findIndex(t => t.id === action.payload)\n      if (index !== -1) {\n        state.toasts.splice(index, 1)\n      }\n    },\n    clearToasts: (state) => {\n      state.toasts = []\n    },\n    setBreadcrumbs: (state, action: PayloadAction<UIState['breadcrumbs']>) => {\n      state.breadcrumbs = action.payload\n    },\n    addBreadcrumb: (state, action: PayloadAction<UIState['breadcrumbs'][0]>) => {\n      // Mark previous breadcrumb as inactive\n      state.breadcrumbs.forEach(crumb => crumb.active = false)\n      state.breadcrumbs.push({ ...action.payload, active: true })\n    },\n    setSearchQuery: (state, action: PayloadAction<string>) => {\n      state.searchState.query = action.payload\n    },\n    setSearchOpen: (state, action: PayloadAction<boolean>) => {\n      state.searchState.isOpen = action.payload\n      if (!action.payload) {\n        state.searchState.query = ''\n        state.searchState.results = []\n      }\n    },\n    setSearchResults: (state, action: PayloadAction<any[]>) => {\n      state.searchState.results = action.payload\n    },\n    setSearching: (state, action: PayloadAction<boolean>) => {\n      state.searchState.isSearching = action.payload\n    },\n    setPanelSize: (state, action: PayloadAction<{\n      panel: string\n      size: number\n    }>) => {\n      state.layout.panelSizes[action.payload.panel] = action.payload.size\n    },\n    setCompactMode: (state, action: PayloadAction<boolean>) => {\n      state.layout.compactMode = action.payload\n    },\n    setShowStatusBar: (state, action: PayloadAction<boolean>) => {\n      state.layout.showStatusBar = action.payload\n    },\n    updatePreferences: (state, action: PayloadAction<Partial<UIState['preferences']>>) => {\n      state.preferences = { ...state.preferences, ...action.payload }\n    },\n    resetUI: (state) => {\n      // Reset to initial state but updatePreferences,\n  resetUI,\n} = uiSlice.actions\n\nexport default uiSlice.reducer"

 id: Date.now().toString(),\n        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()\n      }\n      \n      if (!state.messages[sessionId]) {\n        state.messages[sessionId] = []\n      }\n      \n      state.messages[sessionId].push(newMessage)\n      \n      // Update session\n      const session = state.sessions.find(s => s.id === sessionId)\n      if (session) {\n        session.messageCount = state.messages[sessionId].length\n        session.lastActivity = newMessage.timestamp\n      }\n    },\n    updateMessage: (state, action: PayloadAction<{\n      sessionId: string\n      messageId: string\n      updates: Partial<Message>\n    }>) => {\n      const { sessionId, messageId, updates } = action.payload\n      const messages = state.messages[sessionId]\n      if (messages) {\n        const message = messages.find(m => m.id === messageId)\n        if (message) {\n          Object.assign(message, updates)\n        }\n      }\n    },\n    deleteMessage: (state, action: PayloadAction<{\n      sessionId: string\n      messageId: string\n    }>) => {\n      const { sessionId, messageId } = action.payload\n      const messages = state.messages[sessionId]\n      if (messages) {\n        const index = messages.findIndex(m => m.id === messageId)\n        if (index !== -1) {\n          messages.splice(index, 1)\n        }\n      }\n    },\n    clearSession: (state, action: PayloadAction<string>) => {\n      const sessionId = action.payload\n      state.messages[sessionId] = []\n      \n      const session = state.sessions.find(s => s.id === sessionId)\n      if (session) {\n        session.messageCount = 0\n        session.lastActivity = new Date().toISOString()\n      }\n    },\n    deleteSession: (state, action: PayloadAction<string>) => {\n      const sessionId = action.payload\n      const sessionIndex = state.sessions.findIndex(s => s.id === sessionId)\n      \n      if (sessionIndex !== -1) {\n        state.sessions.splice(sessionIndex, 1)\n        delete state.messages[sessionId]\n        \n        if (state.currentSession?.id === sessionId) {\n          state.currentSession = state.sessions[0] || null\n        }\n      }\n    },\n    setTyping: (state, action: PayloadAction<boolean>) => {\n      state.isTyping = action.payload\n    },\n    setConnectionStatus: (state, action: PayloadAction<{\n      isConnected: boolean\n      error?: string\n    }>) => {\n      state.isConnected = action.payload.isConnected\n      state.connectionError = action.payload.error || null\n    },\n    updateSuggestedQueries: (state, action: PayloadAction<string[]>) => {\n      state.suggestedQueries = action.payload\n    },\n    setConversationMode: (state, action: PayloadAction<ChatState['conversationMode']>) => {\n      state.conversationMode = action.payload\n    },\n    setVoiceEnabled: (state, action: PayloadAction<boolean>) => {\n      state.voiceEnabled = action.payload\n    },\n    setListening: (state, action: PayloadAction<boolean>) => {\n      state.isListening = action.payload\n    },\n    setSpeechToTextEnabled: (state, action: PayloadAction<boolean>) => {\n      state.speechToTextEnabled = action.payload\n    },\n    updateChatPreferences: (state, action: PayloadAction<Partial<ChatState['preferences']>>) => {\n      state.preferences = { ...state.preferences, ...action.payload }\n    },\n    updateSessionContext: (state, action: PayloadAction<{\n      sessionId: string\n      context: Partial<ChatSession['context']>\n    }>) => {\n      const session = state.sessions.find(s => s.id === action.payload.sessionId)\n      if (session) {\n        session.context = { ...session.context, ...action.payload.context }\n      }\n    },\n  },\n  extraReducers: (builder) => {\n    // Send message\n    builder\n      .addCase(sendMessage.pending, (state, action) => {\n        const { sessionId, content } = action.meta.arg\n        \n        // Add user message immediately\n        const userMessage: Message = {\n          id: `temp-${Date.now()}`,\n          content,\n          role: 'user',\n          timestamp: new Date().toISOString()\n        }\n        \n        if (!state.messages[sessionId]) {\n          state.messages[sessionId] = []\n        }\n        state.messages[sessionId].push(userMessage)\n        \n        // Add loading assistant message\n        const loadingMessage: Message = {\n          id: `loading-${Date.now()}`,\n          content: '',\n          role: 'assistant',\n          timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),\n          isLoading: true\n        }\n        state.messages[sessionId].push(loadingMessage)\n        state.isTyping = true\n      })\n      .addCase(sendMessage.fulfilled, (state, action) => {\n        const { sessionId } = action.meta.arg\n        const messages = state.messages[sessionId]\n        \n        if (messages) {\n          // Remove loading message\n          const loadingIndex = messages.findIndex(m => m.isLoading)\n          if (loadingIndex !== -1) {\n            messages.splice(loadingIndex, 1)\n          }\n          \n          // Add actual response\n          messages.push({\n            ...action.payload.message,\n            id: action.payload.messageId,\n            timestamp: new Date().toISOString()\n          })\n        }\n        \n        state.isTyping = false\n      })\n      .addCase(sendMessage.rejected, (state, action) => {\n        const { sessionId } = action.meta.arg\n        const messages = state.messages[sessionId]\n        \n        if (messages) {\n          // Remove loading message\n          const loadingIndex = messages.findIndex(m => m.isLoading)\n          if (loadingIndex !== -1) {\n            messages.splice(loadingIndex, 1)\n          }\n          \n          // Add error message\n          messages.push({\n            id: `error-${Date.now()}`,\n            content: 'Sorry, I encountered an error processing your message.',\n            role: 'assistant',\n            timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),\n            error: action.payload as string\n          })\n        }\n        \n        state.isTyping = false\n      })\n    \n    // Create session\n    builder\n      .addCase(createChatSession.fulfilled, (state, action) => {\n        const newSession = {\n          ...action.payload,\n          isActive: false\n        }\n        state.sessions.unshift(newSession)\n        state.messages[newSession.id] = []\n      })\n    \n    // Load history\n    builder\n      .addCase(loadChatHistory.fulfilled, (state, action) => {\n        const { sessionId, messages } = action.payload\n        state.messages[sessionId] = messages\n      })\n    \n    // Speech to text\n    builder\n      .addCase(processSpeechToText.pending, (state) => {\n        state.isListening = false\n      })\n      .addCase(processSpeechToText.fulfilled, (state, action) => {\n        // The transcribed text will be handled by the component\n        // that initiated the speech-to-text process\n      })\n  },\n})\n\nexport const {\n  setCurrentSession,\n  addMessage,\n  updateMessage,\n  deleteMessage,\n  clearSession,\n  deleteSession,\n  setTyping,\n  setConnectionStatus,\n  updateSuggestedQueries,\n  setConversationMode,\n  setVoiceEnabled,\n  setListening,\n  setSpeechToTextEnabled,\n  updateChatPreferences,\n  updateSessionContext,\n} = chatSlice.actions\n\nexport default chatSlice.reducer"
}
```

'draft',\n          progress: 0,\n          createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),\n          completedAt: undefined,\n          content: undefined,\n          exports: undefined\n        }\n        state.reports.unshift(duplicate)\n      }\n    },\n    updateReportSharing: (state, action: PayloadAction<{\n      reportId: string\n      sharing: Report['sharing']\n    }>) => {\n      const report = state.reports.find(r => r.id === action.payload.reportId)\n      if (report) {\n        report.sharing = action.payload.sharing\n      }\n    },\n    clearPreviewData: (state) => {\n      state.previewData = null\n    },\n    clearError: (state) => {\n      state.error = null\n    },\n  },\n  extraReducers: (builder) => {\n    // Generate report\n    builder\n      .addCase(generateReport.pending, (state) => {\n        state.isGenerating = true\n        state.error = null\n      })\n      .addCase(generateReport.fulfilled, (state, action) => {\n .addCase(exportReport.pending, (state, action) => {\n        state.exportProgress[action.meta.arg.reportId] = 0\n      })\n      .addCase(exportReport.fulfilled, (state, action) => {\n        const {  const { reportId } = action.meta.arg\n        delete state.exportProgress[reportId]\n      })\n    \n    // Share report\n    builder\n      .addCase(shareReport.fulfilled, (state, action) => {\n        const { reportId } = action.meta.arg\n        const report = state.reports.find(r => r.id === reportId)\n        \n        if (report) {\n          report.sharing = action.payload.sharing\n        }\n      })\n    \n    // Preview report\n    builder\n      .addCase(previewReport.pending, (state) => {\n        state.previewData = null\n      })\n      .addCase(previewReport.fulfilled, (state, action) => {\n        state.previewData = action.payload\n      })\n      .addCase(previewReport.rejected, (state, action) => {\n        state.error = action.payload as string\n      })\n  },\n})\n\nexport const {\n  setCurrentReport,\n  updateReportProgress,\n  updateExportProgress,\n  addToGenerationQueue,\n  removeFromGenerationQueue,\n  setFilters,\n  setSorting,\n  deleteReport,\n   "content": "import * as React from \"react\"\nimport { Slot } from \"@radix-ui/react-slot\"\nimport { cva, type VariantProps } from \"class-variance-authority\"\n\nimport { cn } from \"../../lib/utils\"\n\nconst buttonVariants = cva(\n  \"inline-flex items-center justify-center whitespace-nowrap rounded-md text-sm font-medium ring-offset-background transition-colors focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-ring focus-visible:ring-offset-2 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50\",\n  {\n    variants: {\n      variant: {\n        default: \"bg-primary text-primary-foreground hover:bg-primary/90\",\n        destructive:\n          \"bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground hover:bg-destructive/90\",\n        outline:\n          \"border border-input bg-background hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground\",\n        secondary:\n          \"bg-secondary text-secondary-foreground hover:bg-secondary/80\",\n        ghost: \"hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground\",\n        link: \"text-primary underline-offset-4 hover:underline\",\n      },\n      size: {\n        default: \"h-10 px-4 py-2\",\n        sm: \"h-9 rounded-md px-3\",\n        lg: \"h-11 rounded-md px-8\",\n        icon: \"h-10 w-10\",\n      },\n    },\n    defaultVariants: {\n      variant: \"default\",\n      size: \"default\",\n    },\n  }\n)\n\nexport interface ButtonProps\n  extends React.ButtonHTMLAttributes<HTMLButtonElement>,\n    VariantProps<typeof buttonVariants> {\n  asChild?: boolean\n}\n\nconst Button = React.forwardRef<HTMLButtonElement, ButtonProps>(\n  ({ className, variant, size, asChild = false, ...props }, ref) => {\n    const Comp = asChild ? Slot : \"button\"\n    return (\n      <Comp\n        className={cn(buttonVariants({ variant, size, className }))}\n        ref={ref}\n        {...props}\n      />\n    )\n  }\n)\nButton.displayName = \"Button\"\n\nexport { Button, buttonVariants }"

's' : ''}\n              </span>\n            </div>\n          )}\n\n          {/* Loading indicator */}\n          {(loading.global || isRunningAnalysis) && (\n            <div className=\"flex items-center space-x-1\">\n              <Clock className=\"h-3 w-3 text-yellow-500 animate-spin\" />\n              <span className=\"text-yellow-600\">Processing...</span>\n            </div>\n          )}\n\n          {/* Authentication status */}\n          <div className=\"flex items-center space-x-1\">\n            {isAuthenticated ?      \"data-[side=bottom]:translate-y-1 data-[side=left]:-translate-x-1 data-[side=right]:translate-x-1 data-[side=top]:-translate-y-1\",\n        className\n      )}\n      position={position}\n {
  "file_path": "/Users/q284340/Agentic/curriculum-alignment/frontend/src/components/chat/ChatInterface.tsx",

clearCurrentSession,\n  toggleVoiceMode \n} from '../../store/slices/chatSlice'\nimport { Button } from '../ui/button'\nimport { Card, CardContent, CardHeader, CardTitle } from '../ui/card'\nimport { Input } from '../ui/input'\nimport { Textarea } from '../ui/textarea'\nimport { \n  Send, \n  Mic, \n  MicOff, \n  Plus, \n  MessageSquare, \n  Bot, \n  User, \n  Paperclip,\n  RotateCcw,\n  Volume2\n} from 'lucide-react'\nimport { cn } from '../../lib/utils'\n\ninterface ChatMessage {\n  id: string\n  content: string\n  role: 'user' | 'assistant'\n  timestamp: string\n  metadata?: {\n    attachments?: string[]\n    actions?: string[]\n  }\n}\n\nexport const ChatInterface: React.FC = () => {\n  const dispatch = useAppDispatch()\n  const { \n    currentSession, \n    messages, \n    isConnected, \n    isLoading, \n    voiceMode \n  } = useAppSelector(state => state.chat)\n\n  const [messageText, setMessageText] = useState('')\n  const [isRecording, setIsRecording] = useState(false)\n  const messagesEndRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null)\n  const inputRef = useRef<HTMLTextAreaElement>(null)\n  const fileInputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null)\n\n  const scrollToBottom = () => {\n    messagesEndRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' })\n  }\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    scrollToBottom()\n  }, [messages])\n\n  const handleSendMessage = () => {\n    if (!messageText.trim()) return\n\n    dispatch(sendMessage({\n      sessionId: currentSession?.id || '',\n      content: messageText,\n      role: 'user'\n    }))\n\n    setMessageText('')\n  }\n\n  const handleKeyPress = (e: React.KeyboardEvent) => {\n    if (e.key === 'Enter' && !e.shiftKey) {\n      e.preventDefault()\n      handleSendMessage()\n    }\n  }\n\n  const handleNewSession = () => {\n    dispatch(createChatSession('New Analysis Chat'))\n  }\n\n  const handleClearSession = () => {\n    if (currentSession) {\n      dispatch(clearCurrentSession())\n    }\n  }\n\n  const handleVoiceToggle = () => {\n    dispatch(toggleVoiceMode())\n    setIsRecording(!isRecording)\n  }\n\n  const handleFileAttach = () => {\n    fileInputRef.current?.click()\n  }\n\n  const formatTimestamp = (timestamp: string) => {\n    return new Date(timestamp).toLocaleTimeString([], { \n      hour: '2-digit', \n      minute: '2-digit' \n    })\n  }\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"flex flex-col h-full bg-background\">\n      {/* Chat Header */}\n      <div className=\"flex items-center justify-between p-4 border-b bg-card\">\n        <div className=\"flex items-center gap-3\">\n          <MessageSquare className=\"h-5 w-5 text-primary-600\" />\n          <div>\n            <h2 className=\"font-semibold\">\n              {currentSession?.title || 'AI Assistant'}\n            </h2>\n            <p className=\"text-sm text-muted-foreground\">\n              {isConnected ? 'Connected' : 'Disconnected'} • \n              {messages.length} messages\n            </p>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"flex items-center gap-2\">\n          <Button \n            variant=\"outline\" \n            size=\"sm\" \n            onClick={handleVoiceToggle}\n            className={cn(\n              voiceMode.enabled && \"bg-primary-50 border-primary-200\"\n            )}\n          >\n            {voiceMode.enabled ? <Volume2 className=\"h-4 w-4\" /> : <Mic className=\"h-4 w-4\" />}\n          </Button>\n          \n          <Button \n            variant=\"outline\" \n            size=\"sm\" \n            onClick={handleClearSession}\n            disabled={!currentSession || messages.length === 0}\n          >\n            <RotateCcw className=\"h-4 w-4\" />\n          </Button>\n          \n          <Button \n            variant=\"outline\" \n            size=\"sm\" \n            onClick={handleNewSession}\n          >\n            <Plus className=\"h-4 w-4\" />\n          </Button>\n        </div>\n      </div>\n\n      {/* Messages Area */}\n      <div className=\"flex-1 overflow-y-auto p-4 space-y-4\">\n        {messages.length === 0 ? (\n          <div className=\"flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-full text-center\">\n            <Bot className=\"h-12 w-12 text-muted-foreground mb-4\" />\n            <h3 className=\"text-lg font-semibold mb-2\">Welcome to Curriculum Analysis AI</h3>\n            <p className=\"text-muted-foreground max-w-md\">\n              I can help you analyze curricula, compare programs, generate reports, \n              and answer questions about educational content. How can I assist you today?\n            </p>\n            \n            {/* Quick Suggestions */}\n            <div className=\"grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-2 mt-6 w-full max-w-2xl\">\n              <Button \n                variant=\"outline\" \n                className=\"h-auto p-3 text-left\"\n                onClick={() => setMessageText(\"Compare two computer science programs\")}\n              >\n                <div>\n                  <div className=\"font-medium\">Compare Programs</div>\n                  <div className=\"text-sm text-muted-foreground\">\n       className=\"h-auto p-3 text-left\"\n                onClick={() => setMessageText(\"Check ABET accreditation compliance\")}\n              >\n                <div>\n                  <div             </div>\n              </Button>\n              \n              <Button \n                variant=\"outline\" \n                className=\"h-auto p-3 text-left\"\n                onClick={() => setMessageText(\"Generate curriculum gap analysis\")}\n              >\n                <div>\n                  <div className=\"font-medium\">Gap Analysis</div>\n     <Button \n                variant=\"outline\" \n                className=\"h-auto p-3 text-left\"\n                onClick={() => setMessageText(\"Help me understand this curriculum                  Break down curriculum components\n                  </div>\n                </div>\n              </Button>\n            </div>\n          </div>\n        ) : (\n          <>\n            {messages.map((message) => (\n              <div\n                key={message.id}\n                className={cn(\n                  \"flex gap-3\",\n                  message.role === 'user' ? \"flex-shrink-0 w-8 h-8 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center\",\n                    message.role === 'user' \n                      ? \"bg-primary-600 text-white\" \n                      : \"bg-muted\"\n                  )}>\n                    {message.role === 'user' ? (\n                      <User className=\"h-4 w-4\" />\n                    ) : (\n                      <Bot className=\"h-4 w-4\" />\n                    )}\n                  </div>\n\n                  {/* Message Content */}\n                  <div className={cn(\n                    \"rounded-lg p-3 space-y-2\",\n                    message.role === 'user'\n                      ? \"bg-primary-600 text-white\"\n                      : \"bg-muted\"\n                  )}>\n                    <div className=\"text-sm leading-relaxed whitespace-pre-wrap\">\n                      {message.content}\n                    </div>\n                    \n                    {/* Attachments */}\n                    {message.metadata?.attachments && message.metadata.attachments.length > 0 && (\n                      <div className=\"flex flex-wrap gap-2\">\n                        {message.metadata.attachments.map((attachment, index) => (\n                          <div \n                            key={index}\n                            className=\"text-xs bg-white/20 rounded px-2 py-1 flex items-center gap-1\"\n                          >\n                            <Paperclip className=\"h-3 w-3\" />\n                            {attachment}\n                          </div>\n                        ))}\n                      </div>\n                    )}\n                    \n                    <div className={cn(\n                      \"text-xs opacity-70\",\n                      message.role === 'user' ? \"text-right\" : \"text-left\"\n                    )}>\n                      {formatTimestamp(message.timestamp)}\n                    </div>\n                  </div>\n                </div>\n              </div>\n            ))}\n            \n            {/* Loading indicator */}\n            {isLoading.sendMessage && (\n              <div className=\"flex gap-3\">\n                <div className=\"flex-shrink-0 w-8 h-8 rounded-full <div className=\"flex items-center gap-2\">\n                    <div className=\"animate-pulse\">Thinking...</div>\n                    <div className=\"flex gap-1\">\n                      <div     </div>\n                </div>\n              </div>\n            )}\n          </>\n        )}\n        <div ref={messagesEndRef} />\n      </div>\n\n      {/* Input Area */}\n      <div */}\n            {isRecording && (\n              <div className=\"absolute top-2 right-12 flex items-center gap-1\">\n                <div className=\"w-2 h-2 bg-red-500 rounded-full animate-pulse\" className=\"h-4 w-4\" />\n            </Button>\n            \n            <Button\n              variant={isRecording ? \"destructive\" : \"outline\"}\n              size=\"icon\"\n
